namespace = startup

########################################################################################
# startup
########################################################################################
country_event = {
	id = startup.1
	title = "startup.1.t"
	desc = "startup.1.d"
	picture = culture
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_global_flag = game_start_flag }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	immediate = {
			set_global_flag = game_start_flag
			dismantle_hre = yes 

			every_country = {
				limit = {
					government = monarchy
					NOT = { government = tribal }
					NOT = { government = native }
					has_consort_regency = no
					has_regency = no
					NOT = { tag = ASY }
				}
				add_ruler_modifier = { name = ruler_coronation }
			}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "startup.1.a"	
			
	}
}


########################################################################################
# startup - Mrkcosta population sub-mod
########################################################################################
country_event = {
	id = startup.2
	title = "startup.2.t"
	desc = "startup.2.d"
	picture = celebration_priestess
	major = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes		# Debug mode: fire only by console command or through the decision in the human player
	
	#trigger = {
	#	NOT = { has_global_flag = popgrowth_initiated }
	#	NOT = { ai = yes }
	#}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = popgrowth_initiated	# always
		set_global_flag = popgrowth_running		# applies the mod itself, all other events
		
		# here comes the BIG part of the population mod. Basically this gives each province a "province size" that is used to define how much population it can sustain. Then this will be multiplied by any variable that affects agriculture (ie winters, monsoons, aridity); some of those can be offset with technology or certain buildings. 
		# anyway, basically this number is the base "rural capacity" number, so if a province has got value 5, it may sustain 5 rural pops. Higher numbers will cause growth in the province to stop
		# to get this number, I have exported the provinces.bmp map into a program (Imagemagick) that is able to export each color into pixel count, thus showing the province size of each province. After discarding PTI, water, mountains, etc; this is the 1-to-10 scale:
		# 1: 1 to 120 px (only islands and such)
		# 2: 120 to 200 px (delta 80)
		# 3: 200 to 300 px (delta 100)
		# 4: 300 to 425 px (delta 125)
		# 5: 425 to 575 px (delta 150)
		# 6: 575 to 750 px (delta 175)
		# 7: 750 to 1.000 px (delta 250)
		# 8: 1.000 to 1.400 px (delta 400)
		# 9: 1.400 to 2.000 px (delta 600)
		# 10: over 2.000 px 
		
		hidden_effect = {
			
			# Remember to keep updating this database. Last update: 04/05/2021
			1 = { set_variable = { which = prov_size value = 2 } set_variable = { which = prov_id value = 1 } }
			2 = { set_variable = { which = prov_size value = 2 } set_variable = { which = prov_id value = 2 } }
			3 = { set_variable = { which = prov_size value = 1 } set_variable = { which = prov_id value = 3 } }
			4 = { set_variable = { which = prov_size value = 2 } set_variable = { which = prov_id value = 4 } }
			5 = { set_variable = { which = prov_size value = 2 } set_variable = { which = prov_id value = 5 } }
			6 = { set_variable = { which = prov_size value = 1 } set_variable = { which = prov_id value = 6 } }
			7 = { set_variable = { which = prov_size value = 2 } set_variable = { which = prov_id value = 7 } }
			8 = { set_variable = { which = prov_size value = 1 } set_variable = { which = prov_id value = 8 } }
			9 = { set_variable = { which = prov_size value = 2 } set_variable = { which = prov_id value = 9 } }
			10 = { set_variable = { which = prov_size value = 1 } set_variable = { which = prov_id value = 10 } }
			11 = { set_variable = { which = prov_size value = 1 } set_variable = { which = prov_id value = 11 } }
			12 = { set_variable = { which = prov_size value = 2 } set_variable = { which = prov_id value = 12 } }
			13 = { set_variable = { which = prov_size value = 1 } set_variable = { which = prov_id value = 13 } }
			14 = { set_variable = { which = prov_size value = 1 } set_variable = { which = prov_id value = 14 } }
			15 = { set_variable = { which = prov_size value = 1 } set_variable = { which = prov_id value = 15 } }
			16 = { set_variable = { which = prov_size value = 2 } set_variable = { which = prov_id value = 16 } }
			17 = { set_variable = { which = prov_size value = 1 } set_variable = { which = prov_id value = 17 } }
			18 = { set_variable = { which = prov_size value = 2 } set_variable = { which = prov_id value = 18 } }
			19 = { set_variable = { which = prov_size value = 2 } set_variable = { which = prov_id value = 19 } }
			20 = { set_variable = { which = prov_size value = 2 } set_variable = { which = prov_id value = 20 } }

				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { prov_size = 1 } }  add_province_modifier = { name = popgrowth_size01 duration = 30 } }
				else = { set_variable = { which = prov_size value = 1 } 	add_province_modifier = { name = popgrowth_size_no duration = 30 } }
				province_event = { id = population_capacity.1 }
			}
